        <script>  
  var pickingStore = (!$.cookie("picking_store")) ? 73 : $.cookie("picking_store");    
  var pickingStoreVariant = "s:"+pickingStore;
  
  for (var i = 0; i < partsOfStr.length; i++) {
    var variantArray = partsOfStr[i].split(',');
    
    if (variantArray[0].trim() == pickingStoreVariant.trim()){  
      productOfOrigin = variantArray[1];
      var special =  variantArray[2];
      var additional = variantArray[3];       
      var price =  variantArray[5];
      var compareAtPrice = variantArray[6];
      var conversionFactor = $("#product-1954586067003").data("conversion-factor");                               
      var uom = $("#product-1954586067003").data("uom");
      var hideInState = $("#product-1954586067003").data("hideinstate");      
      
      if (additional){        
        $("#product-1954586067003 .additional .sale").html(additional);
        $("#product-19367553564731 .additional").show();
      }
      
      $("#product-1954586067003 .btn").attr('data-id',variantArray[4]);      
      $("#product-1954586067003 .btn").attr('data-cap',variantArray[6]);          
      $(".salecontainer .sale .from_price").html('$' + (variantArray[5]/100).toFixed(2));         
        
      if(special != "Default"){          
        $(".unit_price").addClass("is-special");     
      }
            
      if (!compareAtPrice){
        if (uom != ""){ 
          $(".salecontainer .sale").append('<small>'+Shopify.formatMoney(price*conversionFactor)+" "+uom+'</small>');
        } 
      }
      else{
        $(".salecontainer .sale .compare_at_price").html('$' + (variantArray[6]/100).toFixed(2));              
      }

      if ((parseInt(variantArray[7])<=0) || (hideInState.indexOf(currState) != -1)){
        $("#product-1954586067003 .ajax-add-to-cart-quick").html("<p class='error'>Out of Stock</p>");          
        $("#product-1954586067003 a").css({"pointer-events":"none"});
        $("#product-1954586067003").remove();          
      }
      else{          
        $("#product-1954586067003").addClass("in-stock");

        var items = $("#headercartvals").attr("data-items").split(";");
        $.each(items, function(index, item) {
          if (item){ 
            var itemId = item.split("-")[0];
            var itemQty = item.split("-")[1];
            if (variantArray[4] === itemId){
              $("#product-1954586067003 .btn").addClass("in-cart-btn");
              $("#product-1954586067003").find(".ajax-add-to-cart-quick").hide();
              $("#product-1954586067003").find(".ajax-update-cart .addToCartInput").val(itemQty);
              $("#product-1954586067003").find(".ajax-update-cart").show();                                
            } 
          }
        });                          
      }                
    }                                         
  }  
  setTimeout(function(){                  
    if($("#product-1954586067003:not(.in-stock)").size()>0){  
      $("#add-to-cart-product").hide();
      $("#psalecontainer").html("Out of Stock");
    }                          
  }, 1000);          
</script>
        
        <script>

    var productId =  null;
    var productObj = null;
    
        productId = "#product-1954586067003";
        productObj = $(productId).parent().find('.product-of-origin');
    

    // product of origin second part of the rule
    if(productOfOrigin == "Default"){
        $(productObj).html("Product of Australia");
    } else if (productOfOrigin == "Packaged in") {
        $(productObj).html("Packed in Australia from Imported Ingredients");
    } else if (productOfOrigin == "Packaged in local") {
        $(productObj).html("Packed in Australia from Imported and Local Ingredients");
    } else if (productOfOrigin == "Made In") {
        $(productObj).html("Made in Australia from Imported Ingredients");
    } else if (productOfOrigin == "Made in local") {
        $(productObj).html("Made in Australia from Imported and Local Ingredients"); 
    } else{
        $(productObj).html("Product of "+ productOfOrigin);
    }

</script>

          <h3>Noya Almond Nut Butter</h3>
<p><strong>ALMOND NUT BUTTER<br></strong><em>One of&nbsp;</em><em>the originals, this tasty butter will show you some seriously smooth moves.&nbsp;</em>Premium hand-picked Australian grown almonds, lightly dry-roasted to perfection then crushed and blended, creating a naturally sweet, seriously creamy staple for your pantry. &nbsp;This soft, silky spread is perfect in every meal and on the end of every spoon. Spread it far and wide.&nbsp;<strong><br></strong>--------------------------------------------------------</p>
<strong>INGREDIENTS</strong>
<p><strong></strong> 100% Almonds (lightly dry roasted).</p>
<p>Loved, crushed, naturally. Nothing but nuts, so you can load up your spoon without the trip to guilt town.&nbsp;</p>
<p>Kosher (Certified by KAUST) <br>--------------------------------------------------------</p>
<p><strong><br>HEALTH BENEFITS</strong></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">To keep our bodies healthy, minds happy, we need 30g of nuts every day. That’s just one heaped tablespoon.</p>
<p>Your daily dose of vitamin E, for beautiful hair, nails, and skin, and a powerfully healthier body. Some use vitamin E in skincare, we prefer to eat ours.</p>
<p>Source of protein to keep you fuller for longer, working out stronger, and to help you build muscle, with fibre to keep digestive systems healthy.</p>
<p>Source of healthy fats, naturally low in sugar and sodium to reduce blood pressure. The perfect nutrient booster for you and your folks.</p>
<p>Rich in magnesium, manganese, and copper for a powerful boost of energy. It’s antioxidant rich to protect cells from free radical damage.</p>
Basically, it's the best for healthy bodies.<strong><br></strong>------------------------------------------------------<strong><br><br>NOYA Tick List</strong><br> Rich in healthy monounsaturated fat<br>Trans fat free<br>Naturally low in sugars and sodium<br>Gluten free<br>Less than 10% of an adult’s daily energy needs in a serve<br>All natural<br>Gluten free<br>Dairy free<br>Paleo friendly<br>Vegan<br>No added sugar, salt, oil, additives or preservatives<br>Source of protein<br>Rich in antioxidants: vitamin E, copper, manganese<br>Excellent source of Magnesium<br>Very rich in antioxidant vitamin E one serve gives 100% RDI<br>------------------------------------------------------<strong><br></strong><br> <strong>Don’t just spread the nut; </strong>scoop it.&nbsp;1 heaped tbsp. contains:<br>9.3g Protein&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (19% of an adults recommended dietary intake)<br>11mg Vitamin E&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (110% an adults recommended dietary intake)<br>69mg Magnesium&nbsp;&nbsp; (30% an adults recommended dietary intake)<br>0.21mg Copper&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (30% an adults recommended dietary intake)&nbsp; &nbsp;<br>0.8mg Manganese&nbsp; (30% an adults recommended dietary intake)<br>------------------------------------------------------<strong><br><br>HOW TO USE</strong><br> Straight from your spoon, or alternatively... <br>Drizzled over bananas, split, cut or whole.<br> Mixed in curries and casseroles. <br>Blended in post-workout smoothies.<br> Pretty much everything.&nbsp;<strong><br></strong>-----------------------------------------------------<strong><br><br>COUNTRY OF ORIGIN<br></strong>Made in Australia<strong><br></strong>-----------------------------------------------------<strong><br><br>STORAGE INSTRUCTIONS<br></strong>Store in a cool dry area away from direct sunlight<strong><br></strong>
